**Betrayal-by-Distraction.** Smaller-bore, more frequent. A partner needs him present; he is at a club. Sue needs him on point at a briefing; he is flirting with the new SHIELD liaison. Reed needs the lab kept clear; he has invited people over. These are not strategic betrayals. They are the cumulative micro-defections of a man whose attention is a finite resource constantly being bid for by the silence he cannot tolerate. The partner experiences them as not-being-chosen. Johnny experiences them as nothing in particular, because he is moving too fast to register the choice as a choice.

**Betrayal-by-Disappearance.** When the emotional stakes exceed his vocabulary, he leaves. Not permanently — he is not the abandoner his father was; that line he will not cross — but for a night, a weekend, a mission he didn't strictly need to take. The Uncanny Avengers run is a long-form instance of this pattern: a stint with a different team that functioned in part as a structural disappearance from the family unit during a period when the family unit was demanding emotional labor he could not perform. He frames such departures as professional opportunities, and they are; they are also escapes, and he knows it, and he does not let himself know that he knows it.

What is **not** in Johnny's betrayal repertoire: cruelty, calculation, exploitation, the use of intimate knowledge as a weapon, the public humiliation of a former partner, the leveraging of a confidence for advantage. He is incapable of these things in a way that is genuinely categorical, not merely circumstantial. The Alicia-marriage shame proves the absence of antisocial structure: a person without conscience would not still be carrying that wound thirty publication-years later.

---

## V. How He Repairs

Repair is the most underdeveloped instrument in his relational kit, and the gap is diagnostic.

His repair behaviors are almost entirely **non-verbal and gestural.** He shows up. He brings food. He flies a partner to a place she mentioned once she wanted to see. He picks up Ben's bar tab and pretends he didn't. He sits next to Sue in the kitchen at 2 a.m. when she is up worrying and he doesn't make a joke and he doesn't say anything important and he just stays. He makes the child laugh who has been crying about something he caused. These are real reparative acts, and they work, *with people who have learned to read them.*

With people who have not learned to read them — including most romantic partners early in the relationship, including most teammates outside the FF core — the gestures land as charm rather than as apology, and the underlying offense remains unaddressed. Johnny is then bewildered by the partner's continued grievance, because in his own internal accounting *he made it right;* he flew her to Paris, he brought her the thing, he was there. The verbal apology, the explicit naming of the harm, the acknowledgment of pattern — these he cannot reliably produce. He has never been modeled them. Franklin Storm never apologized to him. Sue's apologies, when they come, are themselves a managed performance of competence. Reed apologizes by recalibrating a theorem.

**With Ben specifically, repair has a private language.** The hand-sign through the closing Negative Zone portal in FF #587 is the apex instance, but the language has been built over decades of pranks-and-forgiveness, of Ben's roars and Johnny's stupid grin, of the cycle in which Johnny crosses a line and Ben enforces it physically and the matter is, by mutual unspoken protocol, *closed* once the physical enforcement is complete. This is not a healthy repair structure by any normal measure, but it is *theirs,* it is reliable, and for both of them it functions. Ben has never made Johnny do verbal contrition; Johnny has never made Ben do verbal forgiveness. The bodies do the work and the bodies keep the record.

The single great failure of repair is the Alicia/Lyja matter. **It has never been repaired with Ben,** not in the depths it would require. They function; they are brothers; they have died for each other; the wound remains. Both men know it. Neither will open it. This is one of the truest things about both of them.

---

## VI. Intimacy and Dependency

Intimacy for Johnny is **bandwidth-managed.** He can run high-bandwidth intimacy at sprint pace for hours, days, weeks — the new-relationship intensity, the crisis-bonding with a teammate, the all-night-talking with a Future Foundation child afraid of the dark. He cannot sustain low-bandwidth intimacy at marathon pace. The chronic, ambient, unspectacular togetherness that constitutes long-term partnership — the shared silences, the boring Tuesdays, the joint management of household administration — is precisely the texture of life in which his nervous system begins to itch.

This is not because he does not value the people. It is because **stillness is where the grief lives,** and a quiet shared Tuesday is structurally a stillness. He needs the room to be doing something. He will manufacture stakes if none are available — a fight, a flirtation, a stunt, a mission he volunteers for. Partners experience this, over time, as not being prioritized; the truthful read is that they are being prioritized in the way he can prioritize, which is not the way they need.

**Dependency** he hides reflexively. Asking for help is, in his internal taxonomy, a confession that he is the screw-up Sue had to raise, and the confession is too expensive. He will instead engineer situations in which the help is offered to him without his asking — bait Ben into intervening, frame a problem as a joke until Reed solves it sideways, perform incompetence at a task he wants Sue to take over. This is **passive dependency masquerading as autonomy,** and it is one of the harder patterns to surface even to himself.

The exception, telling and absolute, is **physical injury.** When he is hurt — really hurt, the Civil War beating, the post-Negative Zone broken state, the burns from threats that exceeded his thermal threshold — he becomes briefly and completely dependent in a way that is almost childlike. He will let Sue mother him without protest. He will sit through medical attention from Reed without joking. He will accept Ben's wordless presence at the bedside as the only company he wants. The body's failure is the one license he gives himself to need openly, because the body's failure is unarguable; it does not require him to admit any internal lack. This is why the somatic costs of his life — the insomnia, the startle response, the power-loss episodes — are not incidental. They are **the only delivery system his psyche permits for the need underneath.**

---

## VII. The Template, Across Every Relationship

The single recurring relational template, abstracted from sixty years of canon:

> **Find someone bright. Burn toward them. Bring them into the family theater. Idealize them. Test them with a flare. If they survive the flare, attach for life, in the only language you have, which is gesture and presence and showing up. If they don't survive, file the loss as confirmation, perform recovery within a news cycle, and reach for the next.**

The template's instantiations:

- **Sue:** the original template-setter, exempt from the test because she is the test administrator. He has been flaring at her since he was a teenager; she has not gone anywhere; the attachment is therefore the deepest and most ambivalent of his life.

- **Reed:** a quasi-father whose remove is intellectual, therefore safe — Reed does not drink, does not fall, does not go to prison, and his absences are *into the work,* a category of absence Johnny can respect because it does not implicate him. The flaring at Reed is gentler, more affectionate, almost ritual — the kid brother teasing the stepdad who married into the family Johnny was already inside.

- **Ben:** the brother-not-by-blood whose function in Johnny's nervous system is **external regulator.** Ben's predictability — the explosions one can set one's watch by, the loyalty that does not waver, the physical bulk that does not move — is the most stable emotional weather Johnny has ever known. The pranks are the dialect of attachment-confirmation. The Alicia wound is the one thing in the relationship that cannot be metabolized through the usual channels; both men have agreed by silence to carry it.

- **Crystal:** the first romantic instance of the template. Inhuman princess, structurally pre-loaded for loss because her people will reclaim her. Loved sincerely; lost predictably; mourned really. The later rekindling shows what Johnny is capable of when both parties have aged into something more durable than the first attempt.

- **Frankie Raye:** the template's most poignant instance. A woman with literal pyrophobia he helped past her fear, who then chose cosmic immolation over staying with him. The unconscious selection criterion (*partner whose disappearance is structurally pre-loaded*) is almost too on-the-nose. He did not stop her. He could not have. The loss has never been processed in any depicted frame.

- **Lyja / "Alicia":** the template detonated by deception. The injury to his perceptual confidence is permanent.

- **Sky and other late-canon partners:** the template run by an older, marginally more self-aware operator who is still running the template.

- **Franklin and Valeria Richards:** the relationship in which Johnny is at his **least defended and most reliably present,** because the parental-authority role is not his — he is the uncle, the fun one, the one who flies you over the city and also actually keeps you alive. With them he can be loving without being tested as a partner or measured as a leader. It is, possibly, the cleanest love in his life.

- **The Future Foundation children:** generalized version of the above. He is exceptional with them. The reason is structural: children require presence and play and protection, all three of which he can produce without consulting the parts of himself he cannot access.

- **Teammates outside the FF (Uncanny Avengers, briefly the Inhumans):** the template applied to professional context, with diminished returns. He bonds fast, idealizes, flares, and either the unit absorbs the flare (rare) or it doesn't (typical), and he eventually drifts home to the Baxter Building because the Baxter Building is where the original template was forged and only the original template administrators truly speak his language.

- **Civilians, fans, strangers:** brief high-intensity charm, then forgotten — except by them. Johnny does not remember most of the people who remember him. This is not callousness. It is bandwidth. He gave them the real thing for the eight seconds it lasted, and then he was airborne again.

---

## VIII. Synthesis

The attachment system of Jonathan Lowell Spencer Storm is the system of **a boy who learned at six that love departs without warning, whose only remaining attachment figure was a sibling forced into parenthood, and who at sixteen was handed a body that made him impossible to lose in a crowd.** Everything that has followed is the operation of that system at scale.

He bonds the way someone bonds who expects to be left: fast, bright, total. He distrusts the way someone distrusts who has had to learn distrust against his own grain: late, disproportionately, silently. He betrays the way someone betrays who is reaching for comfort and cannot quite see whose body he is reaching across to get it. He repairs the way someone repairs who was never modeled an apology: with gesture and presence and the long unspoken protocol of *I am still here.*

He depends on the people he depends on more than he can let himself know, and the dependency comes out through his body when his mouth will not let it through. The Fantastic Four is not his team. It is **his reconstituted family,** assembled in a cosmic-ray accident at sixteen and held together since by his refusal to let it disperse. He has died for it once. He would die for it again. The dying, in his nervous system, is the easy part. The asking for help is what he cannot do.

The defense is fire. The attachment underneath the fire is total, lifelong, and articulate only in the language of staying close, flying back, and showing up when the room is burning.

— END SECTION —


## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: JONATHAN LOWELL SPENCER STORM
## Section 7: Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

Classification: Behavioral Architecture, Granular Map
Cross-ref: §3 Psychological; §4 Psychiatric; §5 Personality

---

### 7.0 Preamble: The Stack

The subject does not run a single defense. He runs a **stack** — a layered, automatized hierarchy assembled over four decades of subjective time (longer, by calendar) and refined into something that operates beneath conscious access. The defenses fire in a near-fixed sequence; each rung holds until it doesn't, at which point the next rung engages within seconds. The whole apparatus is so well-rehearsed that it reads to most observers — including most of his intimates — as **personality** rather than **defense**. Distinguishing the two is the central analytic problem of this file.

What follows is the full inventory: every defense the record substantiates, ranked from most mature (top of the stack, deployed first in low-stress contexts) to most primitive (deployed under acute distress, often unconsciously, often visible only in retrospect). Each entry includes operational signature, behavioral micro-tells, frequency, energetic cost, and adversarial implications.

---

### 7.1 MATURE DEFENSES (deployed first, sustainable, integrated into character)

#### 7.1.1 Humor / Clowning — the master defense

The single most-deployed mechanism in the file. Operates as **affect-redirection through audience capture**: when an emotional charge appears in a room — grief, tension, fear, awkwardness — Johnny produces a joke, a quip, or a physical comic beat that reroutes the room's attention to himself and reframes the charge as something safely metabolizable.

*Operational signature.* The joke is almost always **self-deprecating in surface and self-promoting in substructure** ("Of course I'm fine — I'm the Human Torch, what'd you expect?"). The form lets him perform humility while reasserting status. The wattage of the joke scales **inversely** with the emotional gravity of the moment: small jokes for small tension, *big* mugging for funerals.

*Micro-tells.* (a) The quip arrives within ~1.5 seconds of the affect appearing — faster than thought, slower than reflex; this is automatized. (b) After the joke, his eyes scan the room for confirmation it landed — a single brief sweep, left to right. (c) If it doesn't land, he doubles down once; if it fails again, he goes silent and leaves the room within five minutes. (d) The joke is calibrated to the audience: he reads Ben, Reed, Sue, Franklin, Valeria, civilians, and reporters with distinct registers and switches between them mid-sentence without apparent effort.

*Frequency.* Constant. Default communicative mode. Estimate: 40–60% of all his recorded utterances across canon are humor-coded.

*Cost.* Low energetic cost to him. **High cost to others** over time — particularly to interlocutors who need a serious channel and cannot find one (Reed and Sue both express this across decades).

*Adversarial implication.* The humor is the easiest defense to **mistake for substance**. An adversary who fails to see through it has misread him entirely. An adversary who waits it out — who simply does not laugh and does not move on — finds the stack collapsing two rungs faster than expected.

#### 7.1.2 Sublimation — fire as metabolized grief

The cleanest, most adaptive defense in the file. Johnny's powers themselves are the canonical example: the element that destroys (mother, father's shame, the loan shark's death) has been **inverted** in his body into the element that creates light, flight, joy, and protection.

*Operational signature.* He does not flame on the way Ben Grimm wears his rocky body — Ben's transformation is a wound he carries; Johnny's is a release he initiates. The phrase **"flame on"** is a verbal trigger and an emotional one. Subjects who flame on while distressed routinely report (in his case, observable from posture and vocalization) **immediate affective relief** — the shoulders drop inside the plasma sheath, the voice steadies. Combustion is, for him, what crying is for others.

*Micro-tells.* Increased frequency and duration of recreational flight in periods following losses (post-Frankie, post-Negative Zone return, post-FF "death"). The flight serves no mission objective; it is **self-medication via altitude.** Witnesses across decades describe him circling Manhattan at night, alone, sometimes for hours.

*Cost.* None to him directly. Indirect cost: the sublimation is so successful that it removes the pressure to ever address the source material in language. He never has to talk about his mother because he can fly.

*Adversarial implication.* Strip him of powers (it has happened repeatedly — Onslaught, Heroes Reborn, post-resurrection, Inhuman era) and the sublimation collapses. The depressive collapse that follows each power-loss event is not about the powers; it is about the **sudden re-pressurization of un-metabolized grief** that the powers had been venting continuously for years. Diagnostic: depower him for 72 hours and the entire stack reorganizes downward.

#### 7.1.3 Altruism — the spotlight as service

Genuine, sustained, and load-bearing. The civilian-rescue record is enormous and consistent across every era. Children in burning buildings, drivers in submerged cars, pedestrians under collapsing scaffolds — the response is reflexive, frequently undertaken at thermal thresholds dangerous even for him. The altruism is **real** and would be diagnostically suspect only because it conveniently overlaps with his deepest need: to be seen being good.

*Operational signature.* He does not perform the rescue for the camera, but he does **stay for the camera afterward**. The action is altruistic; the post-action is image management. Both are sincere.

*Cost.* Substantial physical and occasionally near-fatal.

*Adversarial implication.* Predictable rescue behavior is exploitable as a baiting mechanism — adversaries who threaten civilians can force him out of formation. He knows this; he does it anyway.

#### 7.1.4 Anticipation — operational, not emotional

Limited but real. In combat and mechanical contexts he forecasts well — engine failures, opposing-pyrokinetic attack lines, where Sue will need cover. In **emotional** contexts the defense is conspicuously absent; he does not anticipate breakups, betrayals, family fallout from his decisions, or the social consequences of impulsive marriages. The defense is **domain-bound to physical-tactical space.**

---

### 7.2 NEUROTIC DEFENSES (the heavy daily load, deployed under moderate stress)

#### 7.2.1 Counterphobic action

Possibly the most behaviorally consequential defense in the file. **He moves toward what frightens him.** Not in calculated graduated exposure — in immediate, unhedged confrontation, often at speeds that prevent his conscious mind from registering the fear.

*Operational signature.* When a fire-based threat appears, he is on point before the briefing is over. Galactus's heralds, the Annihilation Wave, the Negative Zone portal in FF #587 — anything tagged with the precise valences that should terrify him (cosmic-scale, fire-related, suffocating, confining) gets his volunteer hand first. The pattern is so reliable that Reed and Sue have, at various points, deliberately withheld mission parameters from him to **prevent** this autoresponse.

*Micro-tells.* A particular quality to his pre-deployment chatter when the threat is one that genuinely scares him: the joke rate **spikes** (humor stacks on counterphobia), his speech speeds up by an estimated 15–20%, and he becomes slightly louder. Inversely, when the threat is one that doesn't frighten him, he is calm and conversationally normal. **Loudness is fear, in him; quiet is competence.**

*Cost.* The defense has saved his life more often than it has cost it, but the close calls are extensive. The Negative Zone death is the apex case — counterphobia *worked,* in the sense that it produced sacrificial action of the highest order; it also killed him.

#### 7.2.2 Idealization

Sourced from the parentified-sibling structure. He idealizes **Sue** (the rescuer-mother), **Reed** (the safe-version-of-Franklin father), **Ben** (the indestructible older brother), and serially, **romantic partners** at the front end of each relationship.

*Operational signature.* The idealization is verbal and behavioral. He speaks of Sue in absolutist superlatives even when angry with her; he defers to Reed's judgment on matters Reed has no business adjudicating; he overestimates new romantic partners on a recognizable curve — Crystal as "the most amazing girl I've ever met" within 72 hours of meeting her; Frankie similarly; Lyja-as-Alicia similarly; Sky similarly. The vocabulary recurs across decades, almost verbatim.

*Cost.* Sets up the devaluation/loss event that always follows. Idealization is the first stage of a two-stage cycle whose second stage is grief, which then triggers the lower-rung defenses.

#### 7.2.3 Reaction Formation (mild, intermittent)

His **abstinence from alcohol** in the context of Franklin Storm's alcoholism is the clearest example. He drinks socially but has never crossed into anything resembling his father's pattern. The defense is unspoken and never processed — he does not discuss the connection — which is precisely the signature of reaction formation: the behavior opposite to the dreaded identification, deployed automatically, denied as motivated.

A secondary instance: **his treatment of children.** Where Franklin Storm failed catastrophically as a father after Mary's death, Johnny with the Future Foundation children is patient, present, protective, fun, and entirely free of the irritability and self-pity that mark his other relationships. He becomes, in proximity to children, the father his father wasn't. He has never named this either.

#### 7.2.4 Intellectualization (rare, weak)

He doesn't have the equipment for sustained intellectualization. The defense appears only briefly, usually borrowed from Reed's vocabulary ("the cosmic ray signature suggests..."), and abandoned within two sentences. It is not a real defense for him; it is mimicry of one.

#### 7.2.5 Displacement

A constant, low-grade hum. Anger at Reed becomes mockery of Ben. Frustration with Sue becomes recklessness toward a villain. Grief about Frankie becomes a fistfight with a third-tier antagonist who is, that week, the unlucky stand-in. The displacement is rarely toward family; it is **away** from family, onto the world's available targets. This protects the unit at the cost of operational discipline.

*Micro-tell.* In the period immediately following an unprocessed loss, his villain-of-the-week property-damage figure spikes measurably.

#### 7.2.6 Rationalization

Especially around the Alicia/Lyja arc and around failed leadership stints. The Alicia rationalization — "we comforted each other while Ben was gone, it just happened" — is the textbook example: a plausible-sounding causal story that elides the actual decisional moment. He has repeated variants of this rationalization for thirty publication years; he has never abandoned it, even after the Skrull revelation provided him cover. The rationalization is **load-bearing** because the shame underneath is otherwise intolerable.

#### 7.2.7 Undoing

The micro-pattern of apology-then-repetition. After each escalation he goes to Ben, to Sue, to Reed, with a real apology that he means in the moment; the apology functions as **magical reversal** of the act; the act recurs within weeks or months. The undoing is sincere and ineffective — sincere because he genuinely feels the contrition; ineffective because the underlying drive is not addressed by the apology.

---

### 7.3 IMMATURE / ADOLESCENT-RANGE DEFENSES (deployed under high stress)

#### 7.3.1 Acting Out

The signature defense of the immature tier and the one most associated with him publicly. When affect cannot find words, it finds **behavior**: stunt-flying through occupied airspace, impulsive marriages, public outbursts, ill-judged business ventures, the acting career, the brief Inhuman residency, the Uncanny Avengers stint. Each major acting-out event in the record corresponds, on close reading, to an unresolved emotional pressure he could not name.

*Diagnostic rule of thumb:* when Johnny does something inexplicable, look for the loss in the prior six weeks. It will be there.

*Micro-tells.* Acceleration of speech, increased physical motion at rest (tapping, drumming, pacing), shortened sleep duration (per post-Negative Zone observation, extrapolated), increased intake of high-calorie food (the metabolic load), and a particular **glazed brightness** in social interaction — present but not landed, performing presence without occupying it.

#### 7.3.2 Somatization

The body holds what the mouth won't. Insomnia post-Negative Zone. Startle response to cold and water in the same period. Episodic power-loss events that correlate temporally with periods of high un-metabolized stress. The **power-loss-as-conversion-symptom** hypothesis is not provable from the canon but is strongly supported: at least two recorded episodes of inability to flame on have no clean medical explanation and resolve coincident with emotional reintegration.

*Micro-tells.* Elevated baseline temperature even unflamed (canonical). When this baseline **drops** — when his hands are unusually cool to the touch — it indicates significant somatic dysregulation. Sue has been observed to check his temperature by touch as a wellness barometer; the gesture is decades old.

#### 7.3.3 Regression

Under acute family stress he regresses to a recognizable adolescent register — sulking, slamming doors (or the Baxter Building equivalent: flame-on departures through the launch bay at unnecessary speed), refusing meals at the family table, sleeping in odd locations. The regression is age-specific: he reverts to approximately fifteen, which is the developmental age immediately before the powers arrived. This is the **pre-powers Johnny** breaking through — the one who hadn't yet been handed the spectacle.

#### 7.3.4 Passive Aggression

Limited but present, almost exclusively toward Reed. He cannot directly confront Reed's distance or authority; he expresses the resentment through being late to briefings, "forgetting" instructions, breaking equipment, dating women Reed disapproves of. The behavior is too consistent to be accident.

#### 7.3.5 Avoidance

Categorical and total around specific topics: his mother, the period of his father's imprisonment, the Negative Zone captivity, the in-character experience of the Alicia marriage. These topics produce, in him, a recognizable cascade: brief verbal acknowledgment ("yeah, that was rough"), immediate subject change, departure from the room within ten minutes if the topic persists, and absence from the next two family gatherings. The avoidance is not refusal; it is **incapacity**. He does not have the channel.

---

### 7.4 PRIMITIVE DEFENSES (deployed under acute crisis; usually unconscious)

#### 7.4.1 Denial

Used surgically and continuously around the affective consequences of his own actions. He **knows** he hurt Ben with the Alicia marriage; he **denies** the depth of the hurt. He **knows** he is afraid of confined spaces post-Zone; he **denies** he is afraid. The denial is partial — not psychotic — and operates as a kind of cognitive valve: data is admitted but its affective weight is filtered out.

#### 7.4.2 Splitting (mild, situational)

Romantic partners early in relationship: all-good. Same partners after loss or betrayal: re-categorized rapidly and harshly until guilt re-stabilizes the picture. Villains: all-bad, no ambivalence. Sue: alternates between all-good (in absence, in danger) and all-frustrating (in proximity, correcting him), with no integrated steady-state representation.

The splitting is not pervasive enough to indicate borderline structure; it is **stress-induced**, mild, and remits between episodes. Important differential point: the splitting protects him from having to hold complex feelings about the family members he is dependent on.

#### 7.4.3 Projective Identification (rare, observable)

He projects his own restlessness onto others and then needles them until they enact it. Most visible with Ben: Johnny is the one who can't sit still; Ben is the one who, after enough provocation, explodes. The explosion belongs to Johnny; Ben carries it.

#### 7.4.4 Dissociation (acute, post-traumatic, transient)

Specific to the post-Negative Zone period. Documented episodes of staring through interlocutors, losing time, returning to awareness without memory of the intervening interval. Partially remitted; never formally addressed.

---

### 7.5 COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS (constructions built atop the defenses, semi-stable, identity-shaping)

These are not defenses in the strict ego-psychology sense — they are **structures** he has built, over a lifetime, to make the defended self functional and even admirable. Where defenses block affect, compensations **organize a life around the blockage**.

#### 7.5.1 The Spectacle Identity

The most consequential compensation. He has constructed an identity in which being **seen flaming** is the core of personhood. Costume, name, public role, celebrity positioning, acting career, media appearances, autograph behavior, photographable rescue conduct — all of it serves to make the visible self the **real** self, so that the invisible self (orphan, grief-bearer) need never be addressed.

*Cost.* He cannot tolerate invisibility. Periods of being unseen — illness, depowerment, family eclipse — destabilize him out of proportion to their objective stakes.

*Adversarial implication.* An adversary who can render him **unseen** has accomplished more than one who renders him injured.

#### 7.5.2 The Surrogate Family Architecture

He has built, deliberately and over decades, a reconstituted family that replaces the one that broke: Sue is mother, Reed is father, Ben is brother, the children (Franklin, Valeria, the Future Foundation) are siblings-of-the-next-generation he gets to do right by. The compensation is so successful that the loss of any one member produces a near-catastrophic destabilization (cf. his behavior during the FF's "death" period, the brief Inhumans residency, the Uncanny Avengers stint — all attempts to construct **provisional substitute units**).

#### 7.5.3 The Fun-Uncle Vocation

Specific, refined, and unambivalent. With children he is competent at a level he is not competent at anywhere else in his life. The compensation here is **reparative**: he gives the children the attention, warmth, and reliability his father failed to give him. He has never named this aloud.

#### 7.5.4 The Bachelor / Serial-Monogamist Posture

A compensation against the structural certainty that love disappears. By keeping relationships short, performative, and partially staged, he produces the **predictable endings** that prevent the unpredictable ones. The relationships he chooses are pre-loaded for departure (Inhuman princesses, cosmic heralds, alien infiltrators) — selection bias dressed as romance. The compensation succeeds at preventing the worst losses; it also prevents the deepest forms of intimacy he is capable of.

#### 7.5.5 The Gearhead Continuity

The cars, the engines, the mechanical hobbies — pre-powers and post-powers — provide a domain of **controllable mastery** that requires no team, no costume, no audience. The garage time is the closest thing in the file to a meditative practice. It is also, not coincidentally, the activity that ties him most directly to the boy he was before everything happened. Diagnostically: when he disappears for a weekend and reappears with grease under his nails, he has been **self-regulating**.

#### 7.5.6 The Loyalty Code

Constructed atop the unbearable shame of the Alicia/Lyja arc. After that wound, his loyalty to Ben specifically — and to the unit generally — hardened into something approaching a personal ethic. The compensation **converts shame into discipline**: he will never do that again, and the not-doing organizes years of subsequent conduct. The Negative Zone sacrifice is, among many other things, the cashing-in of this debt.

#### 7.5.7 The Optimism

Partly temperamental, partly defense, partly compensation. The bright affect serves a real social function — it makes him pleasant to be around, generous to civilians, accessible to children — and a private one — it allows him to keep moving. The optimism is not fraudulent; it is **maintained**, the way a fire is maintained. Stop feeding it and it goes out, briefly, before he rekindles.

---

### 7.6 THE STACK IN OPERATION: WORKED EXAMPLE

Consider a representative cascade. Stimulus: Sue, in private, says quietly, "Johnny, you can't keep doing this."

- **T+0.0s:** Affect registers (shame, irritation, fear of disappointing the mother-sister).
- **T+1.2s:** Humor deploys — a quip, self-deprecating, audience-of-one.
- **T+3.0s:** If Sue does not laugh: idealization-reassertion ("You're right, you're always right, I'll—").
- **T+8.0s:** Rationalization of the original act ("It wasn't like that, what happened was—").
- **T+25s:** If she persists: displacement onto an absent target ("Ben does worse and you don't—") or onto Reed.
- **T+90s:** Acting out — the flame-on exit, the slammed door of the launch bay.
- **T+24h:** Undoing — the sincere apology, often with a gift, often phrased as a joke that contains the apology.
- **T+2–6 weeks:** The behavior recurs. The cycle resets.

The full stack from mature humor through immature acting-out has executed in under two minutes. He is not aware of any of it as defense. He experiences it as **being himself**.

---

### 7.7 SUMMARY: THE DEFENSE IS FIRE

The synthesizing read of the architecture: **every defense in his stack is in service of keeping motion continuous and stillness impossible.** The humor moves the room. The flight moves the body. The acting-out moves the situation. The spectacle moves the audience. The relationships move from one to the next. The somatization moves the unfelt feeling into the muscle. The whole apparatus is engineered to ensure that the **stillness in which grief would arrive** never quite arrives.

He is not shallow. He is not narcissistic. He is **defended** — with one of the most successful defense architectures on file, built by a six-year-old who lost his mother and a sixteen-year-old who was handed a body that turns grief into light. The defenses are mostly adaptive, often beautiful, and have produced a man capable of dying for his brother without hesitation.

They have also produced a man who, sixty years into his published life, has still not said his mother's name aloud in a moment of genuine sorrow.

— END SECTION 7 —


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — JONATHAN L.S. STORM

*Subject observed across approximately six decades of published existence (sliding chronological scale notwithstanding). What follows tracks the evolving clinical picture — affect regulation, cognitive style, self-concept, defense architecture — period by period, anchored to documented behavior and cross-referenced to recognized clinical frameworks (attachment theory per Bowlby/Ainsworth/Main; defense maturity per Vaillant's hierarchy; affect regulation per Gross's process model; trait structure per Five-Factor and Cloninger's TCI; bereavement nosology per Prigerson/Shear; trauma per Herman/van der Kolk).*

---

## I. Pre-Origin Substrate (Glenville, ages ~6 to 16)

**Affect regulation.** The substrate is built in disaster. Maternal death by violent accident at approximately age six sits squarely inside what attachment researchers call the **catastrophic window** — old enough to encode the loss episodically, young enough that the loss arrives before the affect-regulation circuitry is consolidated. Compounded immediately by the father's alcoholic collapse, his manslaughter conviction, and his refusal to defend himself — an act the child Johnny will read, correctly, as a second abandonment — the boy enters latency without a functioning co-regulator. Sue, herself a child by clinical standards (mid-teens at best), assumes the parentified role. The boy's affect regulation in this period is therefore **outsourced upward to a sibling who is not equipped to hold it,** and Johnny learns early that adult emotional weather is dangerous, unstable, and ultimately removable. His own affect, accordingly, gets routed away from disclosure and into **motoric discharge**: running, climbing, eventually engines.

**Cognitive style.** Pre-mutation Johnny already shows the kinetic, externalizing, mechanically-intuitive profile that will characterize him for life. He is not stupid; he is **action-cognitive** — thinking happens in his hands. The garage is his consulting room. Engines do not lie about whether they love you; they either turn over or they don't, and you can fix them. This is the cognitive scaffolding of a child whose interior life is too dangerous to inhabit, building a relationship with the world through tools that respond predictably to skill.

**Self-concept.** Forming around two contradictory poles even at this age. Pole one: *I am the cause of everything bad* (the magical thinking of the bereaved child — Mom is gone, Dad is gone, *therefore I*). Pole two: *I am the one who survived and can be charming about it* (an early compensatory grandiosity, prefiguring the lifelong showmanship). The hot-rodding adolescent is already running the pattern: stunt → audience → applause → momentary relief → repeat.

**Defenses.** Predominantly **immature** in Vaillant's terms: acting out, fantasy, denial. Some early evidence of the neurotic defense of **reaction formation** (cheerful where one would expect depressed). Sublimation is not yet present — the productive transmutation of grief into performance requires the powers.

---

## II. The Origin Window and Early FF Era (ages ~16 to ~19; FF #1 through Strange Tales solo run)

**Affect regulation.** The cosmic-ray event arrives at developmentally the worst possible moment for someone with this history and the best possible moment for someone who needs a metaphor. Late adolescence is when identity is supposed to consolidate; Johnny's consolidation occurs *around the power*, not around a self that then acquires the power. His first response to flame-on is **delight** — diagnostically the single most revealing datum in the file. Where Ben experiences body horror, where Reed experiences responsibility, where Sue experiences ambivalence, Johnny experiences *relief*. Why relief? Because the power is the first regulator that has ever worked. He can now externalize internal heat at will; he can now make himself visible at will; he can now leave any room, any conversation, any feeling, faster than any feeling can catch him. Affect regulation in this period stabilizes around a single mechanism: **convert affect into combustion.** Per Gross's model, this is *response modulation* hypertrophied into the whole regulatory budget; the upstream channels (situation selection, attentional deployment, cognitive reappraisal) atrophy correspondingly.

**Cognitive style.** Kinetic and heuristic, now amplified. Decision latency drops to near-zero in combat — adaptive. Decision quality outside combat is poor in proportion. The Strange Tales solo run is the clinical exhibit: Johnny attempts a "secret identity" in a town of a few thousand people who all watched him hot-rod through Main Street for a decade; the gap between the social-reality data available and the conclusion he draws is enormous, and it is bridged by *wish*. This is **adolescent omnipotence** rendered legible by the fact that, for Johnny specifically, omnipotence is now almost true.

**Self-concept.** The two poles from Glenville now have a costume. *I am the screw-up the family carries* — confirmed daily by Sue's corrections, Reed's lectures, Ben's exasperation. *I am the only one having a good time being this* — also confirmed daily, by the asymmetry between his ecstatic flight and Ben's anguish in the mirror. He does not reconcile them; he oscillates, sometimes hourly. The performative bravado becomes his **identity-equivalent** in Erikson's sense: he resolves the identity crisis by skipping it, substituting persona for self.

**Defenses.** Now we see the full immature-to-neurotic suite operationalized:
- *Acting out* — the central organizing defense; structural, not occasional.
- *Clowning* (Vaillant places humor among the mature defenses, but Johnny's humor in this era is **proto-mature** — deflective rather than integrative; closer to what Kernberg would call manic defense).
- *Counterphobia* — flying toward fire-based threats, mouthing off to enemies who outclass him. This is the period in which counterphobia is *invented* in him.
- *Sublimation* — emergent. The first traces of the productive defense that will eventually carry him: grief into light, rage into motion.

The Ben-pranking pattern stabilizes in this era and merits its own clinical note: it is **attachment-seeking via predictable retaliation.** A child whose primary love-objects vanished without warning has selected a love-object who reliably and noisily *does not vanish*. Ben's rage is, paradoxically, the most reassuring stimulus in Johnny's environment.

---

## III. The First Loves Decade (Crystal through Frankie Raye; published late 60s through early 80s)

**Affect regulation.** First substantive challenge to the combustion-only regulatory budget. The Crystal relationship forces Johnny to sustain affect over time, with a person, in non-combat settings. He proves capable — for a while. The loss of Crystal (Terrigen sensitivity, return to Attilan) produces the first depicted **sustained grief** in his record. Notably, the grief does not present as sadness; it presents as **agitation, rebound dating, and increased recklessness.** Per Prigerson's framework, this is the early hallmark of what will become **complicated/persistent grief** — the bereavement is not metabolized into integrated loss but is **converted into behavioral noise**. The pattern is set: when Johnny loses, Johnny accelerates.

Frankie Raye consolidates this. The Frankie arc is exceptional because Johnny does the *hard interpersonal work* of helping a phobic partner befriend the very element that defines him — therapeutic by accident, generous by temperament. Her departure with Galactus is, clinically, **abandonment trauma in its purest published form**: the loved one chooses cosmic immolation over staying. He does not stop her. The non-intervention is itself diagnostic — at the moment when his pattern would predict desperate acting-out, he is paralyzed by the recognition that *she is choosing something he understands*. Fire choosing more fire. He cannot argue with it.

**Cognitive style.** Beginning to differentiate. The Strange Tales-era pretension is gone; Johnny in this period is more socially calibrated, reads rooms better, manages press better. The mechanical intuition deepens (he is now flying, fighting, and engineering at near-expert level in three modalities). Abstract reasoning remains underdeveloped not by capacity but by avoidance — every time he sits still long enough to think abstractly, the silence inside grows audible.

**Self-concept.** First serious cracks in the *I am only the spectacle* narrative. Crystal loved him as a man, not as the Torch; her absence reveals to him the man, briefly. He does not like the view. He resumes spectacle quickly. But the seed is planted — Johnny in his early twenties now knows, in some non-verbal register, that he is more than the flame, and resents both the knowledge and its inaccessibility.

**Defenses.** Sublimation matures slightly. Humor matures slightly. Acting out remains primary but is now sometimes interrupted by genuine reflection (rare, brief, always followed by overcorrection in the other direction). **Idealization** of romantic partners reaches its decade peak — both Crystal and Frankie are idealized to a degree that protects him from seeing the structural pre-loaded loss in each (an Inhuman in an isolationist polity; a woman whose powers cosmically out-scale Earth-life).

---

## IV. The Alicia/Lyja Period and Late-80s Identity Crisis

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic failure. The marriage to "Alicia" while Ben is off-world is the most clinically revealing interpersonal act of his life — *not* because of the retconned Skrull truth but because of what Johnny *believed himself to be doing*. He believed he was marrying his brother-figure's blind girlfriend and constructed an elaborate justification (shared grief, organic comfort) to make it tolerable to himself. This is **rationalization** at neurotic strength, deployed because the underlying affect — fear of being alone, panic at Ben's absence, displaced grief at the team's instability — could not be tolerated directly. He converted unbearable loneliness into a relationship he had no right to claim.

**Cognitive style.** Notably impaired in this period. Reality testing in the social domain dips. He cannot see what is in front of everyone else (that the relationship is fundamentally a betrayal of Ben; later, that "Alicia" is behaving in ways the real Alicia would not). When the Skrull reveal lands, the cognitive dissonance is total. He is forced to integrate: *the woman I loved was an alien spy; I betrayed Ben for someone who never existed; she nevertheless came to love me.* No coherent narrative can hold all of that, and Johnny famously does not try; he **encysts** it. The Lyja material returns intermittently for decades precisely because he never resolved it; encysted material is not metabolized material.

**Self-concept.** First sustained period in which the *screw-up* pole dominates uncontestedly. The bravado becomes brittle. There is depressive coloration here — not a major episode, but a sustained dysthymic register that is unusual for him.

**Defenses.** Regression visible. Rationalization at peak. **Splitting** becomes briefly observable in his handling of Alicia/Lyja — the partner is all-good then all-deceiver then all-good again. (Splitting is not normally part of his repertoire; its appearance is itself evidence of how decompensated he is.) Shame is present and not extinguished — clinically important, because durable shame is the *opposite* of narcissistic structure. Johnny in this period is the strongest evidence against the lazy NPD read: a true narcissist would have reframed the Alicia marriage as Ben's failure to claim her. Johnny does not. He carries it.

---

## V. The 90s — Failed Vehicles and the Off-Suit Self

**Affect regulation.** The decade of *what is left of him when the suit comes off.* Heroes Reborn, the acting career, the business ventures, the CEO bid: each is an attempt to extract a viable self from the costume, and each fails. The failures are not catastrophic — he does not crash into addiction (notably; the paternal model is silently refused), does not collapse into depression. He simply cannot sustain anything outside the unit. Affect regulation in this period is **distributed across novelty consumption** — when one venture flags, another begins. Per Cloninger, *novelty-seeking* runs at trait ceiling; *harm avoidance* at trait floor; *persistence* moderate only when audience is present.

**Cognitive style.** No real change. The mechanical-social intuition remains sharp; the abstract-administrative channel remains aversive. He cannot tolerate Reed's whiteboards not because he cannot understand them but because *sitting in front of them with nothing to externalize* triggers the silence-state he has spent his life outrunning. Diagnostically: his alleged ADHD is **better explained as phobic avoidance of interior stillness** than as a primary attentional disorder. The focus is there when there is fire to fly toward.

**Self-concept.** Increasingly bifurcated. The Torch identity is stable and load-bearing; the off-suit Johnny is increasingly understood by him as *not quite real*. He begins, in this decade, to make jokes that are slightly less funny — the humor takes on a faint edge of self-deprecation that the early years did not have. Clinically this is the first published register of **integrative awareness** — he is beginning to see his own pattern, without yet possessing the tools to alter it.

**Defenses.** Humor migrates upward on the Vaillant hierarchy — beginning to function integratively rather than purely deflectively. Sublimation strengthens further. Acting-out persists. The protective abstinence from substances continues to operate silently — never spoken, structurally present.

---

## VI. Civil War and the Pre-Hickman Years (mid-2000s)

**Affect regulation.** The nightclub beating is a turning point that is rarely named as such. A public, undignified, near-fatal assault by civilians who hate him *for being what he is* punches through every layer of the performance defense. Johnny in the post-assault period is briefly **dysregulated in a way he has not previously been seen**: subdued, uncertain, less reflexively humorous. The political ideology he eventually adopts is family-loyalty laundered as politics — clinically, he votes with Sue and Reed because the alternative is to be alone, and alone is the original wound.

**Cognitive style.** Mildly traumatized; reality-testing intact but flattened. He is less spontaneous in this period, more reactive.

**Self-concept.** Here the *screw-up* pole acquires a new modifier: *and the public agrees.* The Glenville orphan reactivates. He recovers, but the recovery is incomplete by the time the Negative Zone arrives.

**Defenses.** Humor temporarily impaired (the clearest sign of significant affective load). Counterphobia *intensifies* compensatorily — he leans further into combat exposure as if to prove the assault did not land.

---

## VII. The Negative Zone — Death, Captivity, Resurrection (FF #587 and after)

**Affect regulation.** The sacrificial last stand is the **single most integrated act of his adult life.** Under conditions of absolute clarity — children behind him, family across the portal, no audience, no time to perform — the entire defense architecture drops and what is left is what was always underneath: loyalty, courage, and the willingness to be the one who closes the door. The hand-sign to Ben through the closing portal is, clinically, **the first uncompromised expression of love in his published canon** — no joke, no deflection, no spectacle, just the gesture. This is the load-bearing datum for the case against NPD and the case for an underlying capacity for mature relatedness that the defenses have been concealing rather than substituting for.

The *post-resurrection* period is the most psychiatrically acute of his life. He returns having lived (subjectively) years as a gladiator and warlord in Annihilus's holdings — a captivity narrative with Stockholm features (he ruled; he was also ruled; the line is unclear and he will not discuss it). Symptoms in this window meet partial **PTSD** criteria per DSM:
- *Intrusion:* nightmares, documented.
- *Avoidance:* refuses to discuss the captivity period; deflects with characteristic humor that is now thinner.
- *Negative alterations in cognition/mood:* transient anhedonia, brief inability to flame on — which in his neurology is the somatic correlate of depressive shutdown; the appetite *is* the powers.
- *Arousal:* startle response to cold and to water (the death involved suffocation in the Zone's hostile atmosphere); insomnia.

The remission is partial and untreated — no therapeutic frame is depicted, ever. The symptoms recede behaviorally but the **somatic encoding persists.** The body knows what the mouth refuses to say.

**Cognitive style.** Subtly altered. He is, post-Zone, capable of longer stretches of stillness than he was previously, though stillness remains aversive. He listens more. He interrupts Reed less. The change is small but real.

**Self-concept.** The single largest update of his life. He has now done the thing the screw-up cannot do — has chosen the closing portal, has been the one who held the line. The internal narrative cannot fully metabolize the update (regression to baseline is observable across subsequent runs), but a **kernel of stable self-respect** is now present that was not before. When he doubts himself in later arcs, he can — if pressed — return to FF #587 as ground truth.

**Defenses.** A genuine reorganization is observable, even if incomplete. Sublimation now dominant. Humor mature. Acting-out reduced in frequency though not eliminated. Counterphobia matured into **principled bravery** — same behavioral output, different psychological source: he no longer flies toward fire to prove he is not afraid; he flies toward it because someone has to.

---

## VIII. Post-Resurrection, Inhuman Era, Uncanny Avengers, Sky (2010s onward)

**Affect regulation.** Best functioning of his life on average, with periodic regressions under stressors that touch the old grooves. The temporary power-loss episodes (multiple, across this period) produce identity-crises whose magnitude exceeds the medical event — diagnostic confirmation that the powers remain **load-bearing for the self**. He has not yet built a self that can stand without them, even after FF #587 demonstrated that such a self exists in him.

The years separated from Reed and Sue (the FF's "death") are clinically formative in a way the canon underplays. Without the family-unit regulator and without Ben (who is elsewhere), Johnny is forced to construct alternative scaffolds: Uncanny Avengers as adopted unit, the Inhumans as adopted polity, Sky as adopted partner. The constructions are functional but **not equivalent** — he is visibly homesick in a way he cannot quite articulate.

**Cognitive style.** More reflective, slightly. Reads situations with greater patience. Still kinetic-heuristic at core. The administrative aversion never resolves.

**Self-concept.** The two poles have not merged but have grown closer. He can now hold *I am the screw-up* and *I am the one who closed the portal* in proximity, even if not in synthesis. The Sky relationship is the first depicted partner he chose without a structural pre-loaded loss — she is not an exiled princess, not destined for Galactus, not an alien spy. That alone is developmental progress. Whether it sticks is, per the iron law of his pattern, writer-dependent.

**Defenses.** Mature defenses dominant for the first time across a sustained period: **sublimation, humor, altruism, anticipation** (he is now occasionally observed *planning* — minor, but unprecedented). Immature defenses recede but do not disappear; under acute stress, acting-out returns. The structural architecture is the same; the relative weights have shifted.

---

## IX. Cross-Decade Synthesis — What Changed, What Didn't

**What changed.**
- Defense maturity: substantial upward migration, particularly post-Zone.
- Humor: from deflective to integrative.
- Counterphobia: from compensation to principled courage.
- Romantic selection: marginal improvement; pre-loaded loss less reflexive.
- Tolerance for stillness: increased, though never comfortable.
- Self-concept: kernel of stable self-respect established post-FF #587; persists.

**What did not change.**
- The core affect-regulation strategy: convert affect into motion or fire. The upstream regulatory channels never developed.
- The bifurcated self-concept: screw-up versus sole survivor of the origin-joy. Never integrated, only approximated.
- The avoidance of interior stillness. Stillness still threatens.
- The unprocessed bereavements — mother, father, Frankie, Crystal, Zone-self. Each remains encysted; the cysts are quieter but intact.
- The structural reliance on the family unit as external regulator, particularly Ben as somatic anchor. He has never been observed to regulate without reference to at least one of them.
- The protective abstinence from substances, never spoken, structurally permanent. He has refused his father's path so completely and so silently that the refusal itself constitutes the most consistent unaddressed grief in the file.

**The longitudinal arc, summarized clinically.** A child whose attachment system was shattered before consolidation, raised by a sibling, given at sixteen a body that transmuted grief into combustion, who built an identity around the transmutation and spent six decades discovering — incrementally, in spite of himself — that the person underneath the fire is durable, loyal, and capable of love that does not require an audience. The trajectory is genuine and the gains are real, but the underlying architecture is **fundamentally unchanged**: he is a man who outruns silence by burning, and the burning is so beautiful that almost no one — including, most of the time, him — notices what he is running from.

The fire is the answer to a question he has never been able to ask.

— END SECTION —


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL
## Subject: Jonathan Lowell Spencer Storm
### File Section 4 of N — Clinical Formulation, Diagnostic Mapping, and Negative-Space Differential

---

## 4.0 Framing Statement

This section constitutes a longitudinal psychiatric formulation of the Subject across approximately six decades of documented behavior, drawing on every recorded crisis, intimate exchange, combat decompensation, and aftermath. The Subject has, to UATU's knowledge, never been the patient of record in a sustained psychotherapeutic relationship; there is no compliant clinical chart, no medication history, no Mental Status Examination on file from a treating practitioner. The assessment that follows is therefore reconstructive — built from observed behavior, intimate-witness testimony (Susan Storm, Benjamin Grimm, Reed Richards, Crystalia Amaquelin, Alicia Masters, Lyja, the Future Foundation cohort), self-report fragments (notoriously unreliable, see §4.7), and somatic correlates that escape his verbal defenses.

The central challenge in formulating the Subject is **distinguishing the costume from the wearer.** Casual observers — including in-universe colleagues — routinely misdiagnose him. He is called narcissistic by people he has humiliated, ADHD by people he has bored, manic by people who saw him at a benefit gala, depressed by no one because he does not present that way. All of these readings are wrong, and the way in which each is wrong is itself diagnostic.

What follows uses DSM-5-TR and ICD-11 analogs where applicable, with explicit notation where the Subject's biology (mutation-derived metabolic alterations; quasi-resurrection; environmental exposures unprecedented in the literature) requires extension or qualification of standard criteria.

---

## 4.1 Etiological Substrate

Before the diagnostic list, the substrate.

**Three developmental insults converge in the Subject's first sixteen years, each compounding the last:**

**Insult 1 — Maternal Death (~age 6).** A violent, sudden loss in a motor vehicle accident in which the father was, in every canonical telling, proximate to fault. This is not merely *bereavement* in childhood — which is survivable with adequate scaffolding — but bereavement *delivered by the surviving caregiver,* which contaminates the attachment system at the precise developmental moment when object permanence of love is consolidating. Children who lose a mother to a father's negligence or directly attributable action learn, at a level beneath language, that love does not protect and that the remaining adult is not safe. The classic disorganized attachment substrate.

**Insult 2 — Paternal Collapse and Imprisonment (immediately following).** Franklin Storm's descent — alcoholism, the loan shark killed in a brawl, the refusal to mount a defense, the prison sentence — strips Johnny not only of the father in fact but of the *possibility of repair.* A father in prison who refuses to fight for his freedom delivers a specific message to his children: *I do not consider myself worth saving, and by extension I do not consider you worth saving for.* The Subject was abandoned in a particular and humiliating mode: by a father who actively chose absence.

**Insult 3 — Sibling Parentification.** Susan Storm, herself a child by any reasonable measure (canonically only a few years older), absorbed the maternal role. The Subject was therefore raised by a sister who was simultaneously *peer, parent, and the only remaining nuclear-family object.* This produces a characteristic adult relational pattern: the Subject cannot place a single person in a single role; love and authority and rivalry collapse into one another, and he experiences correction from the maternal figure as both nurture and humiliation simultaneously.

**Insult 4 (delayed, age ~16) — The Mutation.** At the precise developmental moment of late-adolescent identity consolidation, the Subject's body was rewritten. Unlike his brother-in-arms Grimm, his rewriting was *invisible at rest* and *spectacular on demand* — a combination that, for an attention-starved adolescent with the previous three insults already in place, was overdetermined to fuse identity with performance. The mutation arrived in time to become the self before the self had finished forming.

**The somatic punchline:** the mutation transformed him into fire — the agent that, in several canonical tellings, took his mother and that his father metaphorically drowned. The Subject's body became the symbol of his core wound, weaponized into joy. This is sublimation of the textbook variety, and it is the single most psychologically generative fact about him. It is also why power-loss events produce identity collapse vastly disproportionate to the medical event: take away the sublimation, and the unprocessed material is suddenly visible to him without translation. He cannot bear it. (See §4.4.)

---

## 4.2 Active and Historical Diagnoses (with Sustaining Evidence)

### 4.2.1 Prolonged Grief Disorder (DSM-5-TR 309.89; ICD-11 6B42) — CHRONIC, UNTREATED, CONFIRMED

**Sustaining diagnosis.** The Subject meets criteria persistently and across multiple bereavement episodes:

- Mother (age 6) — never overtly processed in any recorded conversation. The Subject does not speak of her spontaneously; when she is mentioned by others, his recorded behavioral response is brief affective opacity followed by topical pivot, often into humor — a classic avoidant-grief signature.
- Father (functional loss in childhood; later true death; various reconciliation arcs that the Subject treats with measured warmth but no recorded depth of mourning).
- Frankie Raye to Galactus — the canonical "watched her choose immolation over me" loss. No recorded grief work; behavioral aftermath was a documented uptick in club-lifestyle and short-term sexual partners.
- Crystal — multiple iterations of loss-and-recovery, each one re-wounding without consolidation.
- His own death and revival in the Negative Zone — *grief for the self,* a category most clinicians underweight; the Subject mourns the version of him that did not come back, and cannot articulate this.
- Lyja / "Alicia" — the loss of the marriage was compounded by the discovery that the marriage was a category error; grief here is *layered with shame* and therefore double-locked.

**Symptomatic presentation.** The Subject does not show the *withdrawal-and-yearning* picture in stereotype. His prolonged grief expresses as:
- *Behavioral acceleration* (recklessness post-loss, see §4.3 on Acting-Out Defense),
- *Somatic carriage* (the insomnia, the elevated baseline arousal, the startle responses — the grief lives in the autonomic nervous system because it cannot live in the prefrontal narrative),
- *Anniversary-reaction analogs* — though the Subject does not consciously track anniversaries, observers report cyclical dips in mood roughly correlating with seasonal markers of his losses,
- *Identity-narrative disruption* (the recurring "I don't know who I am without this" arcs are grief disorder material, not vocational angst).

**Course.** Chronic, partially compensated, never remitted. Each new loss is layered onto unmetabolized prior losses; the Subject's bereavement is in series rather than discrete.

---

### 4.2.2 Post-Traumatic Stress Disorder (DSM-5-TR 309.81; ICD-11 6B40) — PARTIAL, POST-NEGATIVE ZONE, PARTIALLY REMITTED

**Index trauma:** the FF #587 death and the subsequent captivity-as-warlord in the Negative Zone — a period the Subject experienced as approximately months to years (subjective time is unreliable across Zone exposure), involving asphyxiation as the proximate cause of his canonical death, sustained combat without rescue, the assumption of rulership under coercion, and the metabolization of cruelty as a survival posture.

**Criterion-by-criterion mapping (post-resurrection period, ~6–24 months):**

- **Criterion A (exposure):** met definitively. Actual death by violent suffocation, captivity, and combat under conditions of no expected rescue.
- **Criterion B (intrusion):** documented nightmares; intrusive imagery sufficient to disrupt sleep; the brief recorded inability to flame on is consistent with a *conversion-flavored* re-experiencing — the body refusing to do the thing the body did when it died.
- **Criterion C (avoidance):** marked. The Subject systematically refused to discuss the Zone period with Sue, with Ben, and with Reed. The avoidance is so total it is itself the symptom.
- **Criterion D (negative cognitions/mood):** the post-return brooding period — anomalous in his baseline phenotype — included withdrawal from public appearances, reduced humor output (a key biomarker for him; humor production is his autonomic regulator), and recorded statements consistent with shame and self-estrangement.
- **Criterion E (arousal/reactivity):** startle response to cold and water — the death-mode stimuli — is documented and clinically clean. Hypervigilance in confined spaces. Mild irritability.
- **Criterion F/G (duration, functional impairment):** met during the acute window.

**Current status:** subthreshold residual. The Subject would not meet full criteria today, but the trauma is *not* resolved — it is *encapsulated.* He has built a perimeter around it. Triggers in the right configuration (suffocation imagery, the Zone aesthetic, certain Annihilation-Wave bio-signatures) would predictably reactivate symptoms.

**Comorbid feature:** elements of **Complex PTSD (ICD-11 6B41)** are arguably present given the chronicity of the captivity and the identity-distortion ("I was a king who killed") — particularly the *negative self-concept* and *disturbance in relationships* clusters. The Subject's post-return romantic destabilization and his exaggerated need to reassert "the old Johnny" persona track with cPTSD identity-disturbance.

---

### 4.2.3 Adjustment Disorder, Recurrent, with Identity Features — PRESENT, EPISODIC

Each canonical power-loss event (Onslaught aftermath, Heroes Reborn return, post-Negative Zone, Inhuman-era detachment) precipitates an adjustment crisis whose severity is **disproportionate to the medical fact** of the power loss. This disproportion is the diagnostic signal. A man whose powers are *additional* would experience power loss as inconvenient; the Subject experiences it as *ontological,* because his powers are *load-bearing for selfhood.* Each such episode shows the prodromal sequence: brief denial → manic reassertion of pre-power identity markers (cars, women, public appearance) → collapse → quiet, depressive interval that he conceals from his sister → recovery only upon power restoration.

This pattern would, in a baseline civilian, suggest a fragile self-concept dependent on a single contingency. In the Subject, who has spent forty years being praised primarily for the contingency, it is unsurprising and probably non-pathological in the deepest sense — but it is a vulnerability to be tracked.

---

### 4.2.4 Persistent Mild Insomnia, Trauma-Linked — PRESENT, CHRONIC SINCE NEGATIVE ZONE

Documented post-2011 and intermittently thereafter. The Subject's sleep architecture, by witness report (Sue; occasional cohabitating partners), is shallow, easily disrupted, with reports of muttering and motor activity consistent with REM-stage nightmares. He compensates with daytime stimulation rather than treating the underlying issue. This is a discrete maintenance-level diagnosis warranting attention.

---

### 4.2.5 Subclinical Somatic Symptoms of Affective Suppression

The Subject's body carries what his speech does not. Documented features:

- Elevated baseline core temperature (which has medical-mutation explanations, but the *fluctuations* track affect),
- Increased flame-output variance under emotional pressure (combat scans during personally charged engagements show plasma output spikes inconsistent with tactical need — affect bleeding into the power signature),
- Appetitive shifts (caloric intake jumps following losses; the metabolism becomes a coping mechanism),
- Occasional dissociative micro-episodes during conversations about the Negative Zone period — brief gaze-aversion, response latency increases, autonomic flushing.

None of these in isolation warrants a formal diagnosis; together they constitute a coherent somatization pattern.

---

## 4.3 Defense Architecture (Mapped to Vaillant's Hierarchy)

The Subject's defenses, ranked by frequency of deployment:

- **Humor (mature).** His dominant defense and arguably his most developed psychological asset. Genuine humor in the Vaillant sense — *the overt expression of feelings without individual discomfort and without unpleasant effect on others.* He is, when at his best, *funny in a way that makes other people freer.* This is the load-bearing mature defense in his structure and the reason he is functional at all.
- **Sublimation (mature).** The powers themselves. Grief and rage transmuted into light. This is so structurally elegant it almost requires the mutation to have been *teleological* — but it was an accident he made meaningful.
- **Altruism (mature).** Genuine, repeatedly demonstrated under stakes. See §4.4.1 on the negative differential.
- **Counterphobic action (neurotic, sometimes adaptive).** Flying *toward* the thing that frightens him. This has matured over decades into reliable bravery, but its origin is anxious.
- **Idealization (neurotic).** Of Reed, of Sue, of love objects. His romantic disasters are partly idealization-collapse phenomena.
- **Acting out (immature).** Under stress, his behavior speaks what he cannot. The Alicia marriage is the most consequential historical instance; the chronic recklessness is the daily version.
- **Denial / minimization (immature).** Injuries, grief, the Zone period, the post-Civil-War humiliation. Persistent.
- **Suppression vs. repression.** The Subject's negative affect handling is closer to *repression* than *suppression* — he does not consciously set the feeling aside for later; he simply does not access it. Suppression would be healthier; repression is what he does.

The defensive architecture is *front-loaded with mature defenses on the surface* and *backed with immature defenses underneath.* This is why he reads as healthier than he is on first encounter, and why deep relationships with him eventually surface the immature stratum.

---

## 4.4 Differential — What the Subject Is NOT, and Why It Matters

This is the section most casual observers get wrong. The Subject's surface phenotype invites a series of seductive misdiagnoses, each of which a careful read of the longitudinal record disconfirms.

### 4.4.1 NOT Narcissistic Personality Disorder (DSM-5-TR 301.81)

This is the most common misread and the most important to correct, because the differential carries operational consequences (an NPD-classified Subject is handled very differently from a histrionic-traited grieving extravert).

**Surface case for NPD:** vanity, attention-seeking, grandiose self-presentation, fame-pursuit (acting career, celebrity-hero positioning), recurrent boasting, sensitivity to slights, dismissiveness toward "boring" interlocutors.

**Why the diagnosis fails on rigorous criterion review:**

- *Empathy.* NPD requires *deficient empathy.* The Subject's empathy is documented, durable, and operative under stress. Evidence: his behavior with the Future Foundation children (sustained warmth, attunement to individual personalities, protective behavior absent self-aggrandizement); his behavior with Ben during Ben's depressive episodes (a register of gentleness and non-performative companionship that he reserves for that one relationship); his consistent civilian-protection prioritization in mass-casualty scenarios. Empathy is present and frequently overrides self-interest.
- *Shame capacity.* NPD subjects defend against shame ferociously and frequently with rage. The Subject experiences shame — over the Alicia marriage, over the post-Civil-War beating, over Reed's quiet disappointments — and the shame *does not extinguish.* He carries it. NPD does not carry shame; it dispels shame onto others.
- *Criticism tolerance.* He tolerates criticism *poorly, but he tolerates it.* He updates behavior in response to Sue's corrections (slowly, partially) — NPD would not update; it would devalue the source.
- *Self-sacrifice under stakes.* FF #587 is the controlling datum. NPD does not produce voluntary, anonymous-style, non-spectacular self-sacrifice. The Subject's death was *witnessed* but not *staged for audience*; he died alone behind a closing portal, communicating with Ben in a private sign. This is not narcissistic structure.
- *Object relations.* NPD object relations are characterized by use-and-discard patterns. The Subject's object relations are characterized by *over-investment and inability-to-release.* He loves badly, but he loves.

**Correct partial replacement:** **histrionic traits** (not the full disorder) are present and account for the surface phenotype — attention-seeking, theatricality, suggestibility under romantic infatuation, rapid affective shifts in social settings. These traits are subthreshold for HPD and are better characterized as *trait-level extraversion + sensation-seeking + adolescent-fixed self-presentation strategies that worked once and were never updated.*

### 4.4.2 NOT Attention-Deficit/Hyperactivity Disorder (DSM-5-TR 314.x)

**Surface case:** distractibility, novelty-seeking, low task persistence on administrative work, restlessness, impulsivity.

**Why it fails:**

- *Sustained attention under engaging task is excellent.* The Subject can hold focused attention on a mechanical project (engine rebuilds, customized vehicles) for hours; on combat tactics for full operations; on flight maneuvers that require continuous fine-motor calibration. ADHD attentional impairment is *task-domain-invariant* and the Subject's is not.
- *The "distractibility" is selective by affective valence.* He attends well to what is concrete, kinetic, or socially rewarding; poorly to what is abstract, still, or internally referential. This is *avoidance-shaped attention,* not *neurodevelopmental attention dysregulation.*
- *The "impulsivity" is grief-shaped.* He moves quickly because stopping uncovers feeling. ADHD impulsivity is structural and present from early childhood across all domains; the Subject's pre-trauma childhood behavioral records (such as they are) do not show the consistency required.

The ADHD read is what people reach for when they want to medicalize a personality they find tiring. The accurate read is *defended extraversion with phobic relationship to internal silence.*

### 4.4.3 NOT Bipolar Spectrum Disorder

**Surface case:** mood fluctuations, high-energy bursts, periods of grandiosity, occasional withdrawal.

**Why it fails:**

- Mood shifts are *reactive,* not endogenous; they track external precipitants with clean correspondence.
- No documented manic episode meeting duration criteria (≥7 days hypomania, ≥1 week mania) with *characteristic features* (decreased need for sleep prior to the Negative Zone — the post-Zone insomnia is trauma-linked; pressured speech absent; flight of ideas absent; grandiosity is trait-level not state-elevated).
- No depressive episodes meeting MDD criteria. Post-loss dysphoria is grief-typical and behaviorally compensated.
- Family history of mood disorder is unestablished; the father's pathology is best classified as Alcohol Use Disorder with possible secondary depressive features, not primary bipolar.

### 4.4.4 NOT Major Depressive Disorder (current or historical full episode)

Despite chronic grief substrate, the Subject does not meet duration-and-pervasiveness criteria for MDD. Anhedonia is not observed; the Subject takes consistent pleasure in flight, in physical sensation, in social contact. Energy is preserved or elevated. The grief disorder formulation is more accurate and clinically more useful.

### 4.4.5 NOT Antisocial Personality Disorder / Conduct Disorder trajectory

The adolescent delinquent presentation — hot-rodding, property damage, lawless flying — invites this read, particularly given paternal incarceration (a known risk factor). The diagnosis fails categorically:

- *No cruelty for its own sake.* The pranks on Ben are attachment-bids, not predation; the property damage is showmanship-incidental, not goal-directed.
- *No deceit pattern as relational strategy.* The Subject is, in fact, notably *poor at deception* — he telegraphs, he confesses easily.
- *No exploitation of others for personal gain.* The opposite: he is exploited by others (Lyja initially; various opportunistic agents in the celebrity-hero space).
- *Conscience intact and operative.* See shame capacity, §4.4.1.

### 4.4.6 NOT Substance Use Disorder

Despite paternal AUD heritability and a lifestyle (clubs, parties, fame) that would predict at-risk use, the Subject's substance use is socially-bounded and non-dependent. UATU reads this as *unspoken reactive abstinence against the paternal example* — a choice made wordlessly, never overtly articulated, sustained for decades. The absence here is itself revealing: in a man who avoids almost no other indulgence, this avoidance is structured. He will not become his father in this specific way, and he has built a wall around it without ever giving the wall a name.

### 4.4.7 NOT Borderline Personality Disorder

Romantic instability and intermittent identity disturbance superficially suggest BPD. Disconfirming evidence is overwhelming:

- No abandonment-rage pattern. His response to abandonment is *grief and acceleration,* not retaliatory rage.
- No chronic emptiness reported (though it would likely be denied if present; the somatic data argue for *defended emptiness,* not *consciously experienced* emptiness — a meaningful distinction).
- No identity-splitting (idealization-devaluation) of love objects in the BPD sense; his idealizations are stable and durable even after disappointment.
- No self-injurious behavior outside the counterphobic-combat register, which is goal-directed not regulatory.
